INC-SPECT  .Monoenergetic 60.5 - 61.9 +/- 0.1 and 38.7 +/- 0.1 MeVO0290  1   13 
            protons, focused on the target in a spot of approxi-  O0290  1   14 
            mately 8 mm diameter, with a walk of +/- 0.4 cm. The  O0290  1   15 
            uncertainty in number of protons striking the target  O0290  1   16 
            was +/- 1%.                                           O0290  1   17 
METHOD     (EDE) The secondary particle type was identified with  O0290  1   18 
           (TOF) A combination of delta-E versus E and Flight-TimeO0290  1   19 
           versus E, which permitted unambiguous identification   O0290  1   20 
           from a few MeV up to 62 MeV. The low-energy            O0290  1   21 
           cutoffs for the different particles were               O0290  1   22 
           -------------------------------------------------------O0290  1   23 
             61.7 MeV                                             O0290  1   24 
                  Protons       15 -  45 degrees    6 - 9 MeV     O0290  1   25 
                                50 - 135 degrees        4 MeV     O0290  1   26

                  Deuterons     15 - 135 degrees        5 MeV     O0290  1   28 
                                     160 degrees       11 MeV     O0290  1   29 
                  Tritons       15 - 135 degrees        6 MeV     O0290  1   30

DETECTOR   (TELES,SIBAR,GELI) A solid state three-detector        O0290  1   42 
            telescope, with two silicon surface-barrier delta-E   O0290  1   43 
            detectors about 100 and 500 mu-m in thickness and a   O0290  1   44 
            lithium-drifted germanium detector used for total     O0290  1   45 
            energy absorption. The total resolution was           O0290  1   46 
            approximately 180 keV for most of the data.           O0290  1   47 
            The telescope was mounted in a scattering chamber withO0290  1   48 
            1.2 m diameter. For the runs at 61.7 MeV, nickel      O0290  1   49 
            collimators with a thickness of 0.653 cm and areas of O0290  1   50 
            0.173 - 0.259 cm2 +/- 1.5 %, was used. For the        O0290  1   51 
            runs at 38.7 MeV an active NE102 collimator, with a   O0290  1   52 
            thickness of 0.1 cm and an area of 0.342 cm2 +/- 1.5%,O0290  1   53 
            was used. The distance from the target to the         O0290  1   54 
            collimator was about 47 cm +/- 1%. The collimator     O0290  1   55 
            had a misalignment at the center of the scattering    O0290  1   56 
            chamber of +/- 0.5 cm. The precision of the detector  O0290  1   57 
            angle was +/- 0.5 degrees. The zero angle was         O0290  1   58 
            determined to +/- 0.5 degrees. The angular resolution O0290  1   59 
            was better than +/- 0.45 degrees.                     O0290  1   60 
SAMPLE     .Bismuth target, 10.3 +/- 0.2 mg/cm2 thick, with a     O0290  1   61 
            thickness nonuniformity of +/- 3 %. The target        O0290  1   62 
            contained 0.20 +/- 0.02 atom % carbon and             O0290  1   63 
            0.30 +/- 0.04 atom % oxygen. The sample was           O0290  1   64 
            oriented with an angular precision of +/- 0.5 degrees.O0290  1   65 
CORRECTION .The data were corrected for                           O0290  1   66 
            1. Energy loss of the secondary particles in the      O0290  1   67 
               target,                                            O0290  1   68 
            2. Collimator edge penetration,                       O0290  1   69 
            3. Multiple scattering of particles in the first two  O0290  1   70 
               detectors, which made them miss the total absorp-  O0290  1   71 
               tion detector,                                     O0290  1   72 
            4. The nickel window dead layer of the Ge-detector,   O0290  1   73 
               and,                                               O0290  1   74 
            5. Nuclear reactions in the Ge-Detector.              O0290  1   75
